\hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__MPM_ga9f5959dd76d5c83e775dcf44de684686}{        result} += 1; \hyperlink{group__apr__env_ga711ebc0efad43aba10f32ded4a28cf17}{\(\backslash\)}
\hyperlink{group__apr__env_ga711ebc0efad43aba10f32ded4a28cf17}{        value} >>= 1; \(\backslash\)
    \}
\end{DoxyCode}
